<div id="ctr_stuff_before_server_form" name="ctr_stuff_before_server_form"><h3>Competitions used in ranking&nbsp;<a href='?a=327&ladder_id=3&ranking_date=2017-09-01&ctype=excel'><image style='border:none' src='img/excel.png' alt='Excel' height='10px'/></a></h3><i>Notes:<br />A new ranking is created just after midnight UTC on the 1st every month.<br />This (current) ranking is then updated every day around midnight UTC with any new results registered (for comps ending prior to the ranking date).<br />Once a new ranking is created the previous month's ranking will be "frozen". It is considered history with whatever errors there may be.<br />It is everyones responsibility to check the rankings and notify <a href='http://www.fai.org/hang_gliding/EmailCIVL'>CIVL</a> of any errors. From the ranking is created on the 1st one has a full month to discover any errors.<br /><br />To organizers:<br />It is your responsibility to follow up after sending results to CIVL. If you do not receive confirmation that the results has been received within a few days after submitting results you should check the ranking and contact <a href='http://www.fai.org/hang_gliding/EmailCIVL'>CIVL</a>.<br />In order for results to be included in a ranking, CIVL should have received the results as soon as possible after the competition is finished.<br /> If we receive the results after the middle of the current ranking month we cannot guarantee that they will be included in this month's ranking.<br /><br />If the dates in the first column is red it means results has not yet been registered.<br />If the date in the last column is red it means the results has been registered (or updated) since last time the ranking was updated. If this is the current (last) ranking, it will be updated within 24 hours.<br /><br /></i><p>Number of competitions: 440</p>&nbsp;<a href='?a=326&ladder_id=3&ranking_date=2017-09-01&'>Pilots ranking</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href='?a=328&ladder_id=3&ranking_date=2017-09-01&'>Nations ranking</a>&nbsp;<br /><br /></div>
